###########################
# Canada Events
###########################

add_namespace = canada

# Intro events
country_event = {
	id = canada.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.1" }
	title = canada.1.t
	desc = canada.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_canada_map

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = canada.2 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = canada.4 days = 18 } #Death of George V
			country_event = { id = canada.24 days = 73 } #Call for election
			country_event = { id = canada.20 days = 98 } #1936 Stanley Cup
			country_event = { id = canada.29 days = 237 } #Duplessis becomes Premier of Quebec
			country_event = { id = canada.72 days = 1095 random = 4320 } #J.S. Woodsworth loses CCF leadership to Coldwell
			country_event = { id = canada.70 days = 2928 } #Mackenzie King Retires
			country_event = { id = canada.71 days = 3289 } #R.B. Bennett Retires
		}
	}
}

# Death of King George V
country_event = {
	id = canada.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.4" }
	title = canada.4.t
	desc = canada.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_death_george

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = { name = "George V" ruling_only = yes }
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.4.a
		clr_global_flag = CAN_king_george_V
		set_global_flag = CAN_king_edward_VIII
		set_country_flag = CAN_king_coronation_pending
		set_variable = { king_popularity = 2 }
		set_variable = { global.king_edward_story = 0 }
		add_stability = -0.05
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_king_speech_unlocked
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN_create_monarchy = yes
			# official coronation
			country_event = { id = canada.5 days = 90 }
			# country-specific death events
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = DEH }
				DEH = { country_event = delhi.3 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = NFA }
				NFA = { 
					country_event = {
						id = nfa.4 
						days = 2 
					}
				}
			}
			NFL = {
				country_event = newfoundland.2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = AST }
				AST = { country_event = austral.3 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = TRM }
				TRM = { country_event = tram.125 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = IRE }
				IRE = { country_event = irelandflavour.200 }
			}
			# main news events
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = { id = worldnews.28 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Coronation of King Edward
country_event = {
	id = canada.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.5" }
	title = canada.5.t
	desc = canada.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_coronation

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = { name = "Edward VIII" ruling_only = yes }
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.5.a
		add_stability = 0.05
		clr_global_flag = CAN_king_busy
		clr_country_flag = CAN_king_coronation_pending
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_king_coronated
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_king_popularity_increase
		add_to_variable = { king_popularity = 1 }
		CAN_calc_royal_visit_effects = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = entente.50 days = 60 } #begin random royal events
			country_event = { id = canada.447 days = 34 random_days =11 } #Crown Royal
		}
	}
}

# The King's First Address
country_event = {
	id = canada.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.6" }
	title = canada.6.t
	desc = canada.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_edward2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.6.a #He will prepare the nation for war
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_address_war
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = canada.7 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.6.b #He will endorse the Conservatives
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_address_cons
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = canada.7 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.6.c #He will support the Canadian government
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_address_gov
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = canada.7 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# Results of the Address
country_event = {
	id = canada.7
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.7" }
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_microphone

	title = {
		text = canada.7.t.war
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_address_war }
	}
	title = {
		text = canada.7.t.cons
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_address_cons }
	}
	title = {
		text = canada.7.t.gov
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_address_gov }
	}

	desc = {
		text = canada.7.d.war
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_address_war }
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.7.d.cons
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_address_cons }
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.7.d.gov
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_address_gov }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.7.a #We must liberate our brothers in Britain!
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_address_war }
		clr_country_flag = CAN_address_war
		add_war_support = 0.10
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { king_influence < 5 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_exile_influence_increase
			add_to_variable = { king_influence = 1 }
			CAN_calc_exile_influence_effects = yes
		}
		CAN_improve_exile_influence_small_bop = yes
		add_to_variable = { CAN_conservative_support = 1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 }
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.7.b #This election will be vital for our future!
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_address_cons }
		clr_country_flag = CAN_address_cons
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = 50
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { king_popularity < 5 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_king_popularity_increase
			add_to_variable = { king_popularity = 1 }
			CAN_calc_royal_visit_effects = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { CAN_conservative_support = 2 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.7.c #The 20th century shall be Canada's Century!
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_address_gov }
		clr_country_flag = CAN_address_gov
		add_to_variable = { CAN_liberal_support = 1 }
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = 0.03
		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
	}
}

# Status of the Privy Council (fired by focus)
country_event = {
	id = canada.8
	title = canada.8.t
	desc = canada.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_prime_minister

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.8"
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = CAN_Douglas_Hogg_lobe_ade
			GBR = { clr_country_flag = GBR_Hogg_PM }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.8.a #Let the king pick his replacement
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = GBR_return_of_the_king
					option = GBR_RETURN_OF_THE_KING_DEMOCRACY_SOCCON
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_liberal_government = yes
				check_variable = { CAN_liberal_support < 1 }
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		GBR = { set_country_flag = GBR_Croft_PM }
		add_ideas = CAN_Henry_Page_Croft_lobe_pau
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { king_influence < 5 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_exile_influence_increase
			add_to_variable = { king_influence = 1 }
			CAN_calc_exile_influence_effects = yes
		}
		CAN_improve_exile_influence_bop = yes
		add_to_variable = { CAN_conservative_support = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.8.b #We should push for a moderate candidate
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GBR_return_of_the_king
						option = GBR_RETURN_OF_THE_KING_DEMOCRACY_AUTDEM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GBR_return_of_the_king
						option = GBR_RETURN_OF_THE_KING_AUTDEM
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_government = social_conservative
				check_variable = { CAN_conservative_support > 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_government = social_conservative
				check_variable = { CAN_conservative_support < 1 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.81
				days = 600
				random_days = 200
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		GBR = { set_country_flag = GBR_Cecil_PM }
		add_ideas = CAN_Robert_Cecil_lobe_ade
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { king_influence > 0 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_exile_influence_decrease
			subtract_from_variable = { king_influence = 1 }
			CAN_calc_exile_influence_effects = yes
		}
		CAN_improve_canadian_influence_bop = yes
		add_to_variable = { CAN_liberal_support = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.8.c #A vote by the Exiles should be organized
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GBR_return_of_the_king
						option = GBR_RETURN_OF_THE_KING_DEMOCRACY_AUTDEM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GBR_return_of_the_king
						option = GBR_RETURN_OF_THE_KING_AUTDEM
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.81
				days = 600
				random_days = 200
			}
		}
		GBR = { set_country_flag = GBR_Halifax_PM }
		add_ideas = CAN_Edward_Halifax_lobe_sco
		add_stability = 0.03
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.8.e #A vote by the Exiles should be organized
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GBR_return_of_the_king
						option = GBR_RETURN_OF_THE_KING_DEMOCRACY_AUTDEM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GBR_return_of_the_king
						option = GBR_RETURN_OF_THE_KING_AUTDEM
					}
				}
			}
		}
		GBR = { set_country_flag = GBR_Baldwin_PM }
		add_ideas = CAN_Stanley_Baldwin_lobe_ade
		add_stability = 0.03
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.80
				days = 400
				random_days = 120
			}
			country_event = {
				id = canada.81
				days = 600
				random_days = 200
			}
		}
	}
}

# Baldwin Resigns
country_event = {
	id = canada.80
	title = canada.80.t
	desc = canada.80.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_stanley_baldwin

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.8"
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = CAN_Stanley_Baldwin_lobe_ade
			GBR = { clr_country_flag = GBR_Baldwin_PM }
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_idea = CAN_Stanley_Baldwin_lobe_ade
		has_global_flag = CAN_king_edward_VIII
		CAN_has_elections = yes
	}

	option = { #Halifax
		name = canada.80.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
		add_ideas = CAN_Edward_Halifax_lobe_sco
	}
	
	option = { #Chamberlain
		name = canada.80.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
		add_ideas = CAN_Neville_Chamberlain_lobe_ade
		GBR = {
			set_country_flag = GBR_Chamberlain_PM
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Eden
		name = canada.80.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
		add_ideas = CAN_Anthony_Eden_lobe_ade

		}

}

# Exile Vote?
country_event = {
	id = canada.81
	title = canada.81.t
	desc = canada.81.d
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.81" }
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_exiles_vote

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		CAN_has_elections = yes
	}

	option = { #They Have Enough Influence Already
		name = canada.81.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = -0.05
		CAN_improve_canadian_influence_small_bop = yes
	}
	
	option = { #Own Elections
		name = canada.81.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.82
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Allow Vote
		name = canada.81.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.10
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		CAN_improve_exile_influence_bop = yes
	}
}

# Fate of the Senate (fired by focus)
country_event = {
	id = canada.9
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.9" }
	title = canada.9.t
	desc = canada.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_senate

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.9.a #We need reform at once!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = canada.1010
			days = 2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.9.b #Urge the king to pick Canadians
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_stability = 0.03
		add_political_power = 50
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.9.c #It's the king's prerogative to choose as he wishes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_liberal_government = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_restored_senate
		add_political_power = 100
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.10 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { king_influence < 5 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_exile_influence_increase
			add_to_variable = { king_influence = 1 }
			CAN_calc_exile_influence_effects = yes
		}
		CAN_improve_exile_influence_bop = yes
		add_to_variable = { CAN_conservative_support = 1 }
	}
}

# The Senate Bill
country_event = {
	id = canada.1010
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.1010" }
	title = canada.1010.t
	desc = canada.1010.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_commons2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Refuse
		name = canada.1010.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		country_event = {
			id = canada.10
			days = 2
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Accept
		name = canada.1010.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		country_event = {
			id = canada.11
			days = 2
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_restored_senate
	}
}

# The Senate refuses the bill

# The Senate agrees to the bill
country_event = {
	id = canada.11
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.11" }
	title = canada.11.t
	desc = canada.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_senate2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.11.a
		set_country_flag = CAN_restored_senate
		set_country_flag = CAN_has_senate_reform
		add_political_power = 100
		add_to_variable = { CAN_liberal_support = 1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = -0.05 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { king_influence > 0 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_exile_influence_decrease
			subtract_from_variable = { king_influence = 1 }
			CAN_calc_exile_influence_effects = yes
		}
		CAN_improve_canadian_influence_bop = yes
	}
}

		OR = {
			tag = CAN
			tag = USA
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.20.a
		trigger = { tag = CAN }
		hidden_effect = {

				}

					country_event = { id = canada.22 days = 2 } #Toronto wins
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.20.b
		trigger = { tag = USA }
	}
}

# Black Monday hits Canada
country_event = {
	id = canada.23
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.23" }
	title = canada.23.t
	desc = canada.23.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_great_depression

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.23.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_great_depression_3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_great_depression_3
				add_idea = CAN_great_depression_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_great_depression_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_great_depression_2
				add_idea = CAN_great_depression_1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = CAN_great_depression_3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.240
				days = 12
			}
			NFL = {
				country_event = newfoundland.3
			}
		}
	}
}

# Canada at war prior to the elections
country_event = {
	id = canada.33
	title = canada.33.t
	desc = canada.33.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_edward3

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		has_war = yes
		CAN_has_elections = yes
		has_country_flag = KR_british_king_base
		NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_had_1936_election }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.33"
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = CAN
					OR = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction = no
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = war_country
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.33.a
		add_to_variable = { CAN_conservative_support = 1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 }
	}
}

# Complaints about conditions at labour camps (triggered by focus)
country_event = {
	id = canada.34
	title = canada.34.t
	desc = canada.34.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_camp

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = CAN_work_camps
			has_idea = CAN_work_camps_2
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.34"
		hidden_effect = {
			
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.34.a # Shut down the camps
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_liberal_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		set_country_flag = CAN_camps_shut_down
		add_political_power = 25
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_work_camps }
			remove_ideas = CAN_work_camps
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_work_camps_2 }
			remove_ideas = CAN_work_camps_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.34.b # Improve conditions
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		add_political_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_work_camps_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_work_camps_2
				add_idea = CAN_work_camps
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = canada.35 days = 730 random = 1440 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.34.c # These men should be grateful!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_liberal_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
			}
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5  = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = canada.35 days = 365 random = 1440 }
		}
	}
}

# The 'March on Ottawa'
country_event = {
	id = canada.35
	title = canada.35.t
	desc = canada.35.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_camp

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = CAN_work_camps
			has_idea = CAN_work_camps_2
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.35"
		hidden_effect = {
			decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.35.a # Shut down the camps
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_liberal_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_camps_shut_down
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_work_camps }
			remove_ideas = CAN_work_camps
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_work_camps_2 }
			remove_ideas = CAN_work_camps_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.35.b # Improve conditions
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_liberal_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_camps_not_shut_down
		add_political_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_work_camps_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_work_camps_2
				add_idea = CAN_work_camps
			}
		}
	}
}

# Unemployment Insurance proposed
country_event = {
	id = canada.36
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.36" }
	title = canada.36.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_camp

	desc = {
		text = canada.36.d.camps
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_camps_not_shut_down }
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.36.d.nocamps
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_camps_shut_down }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		date > 1940.1.1
		OR = {
			has_liberal_government = yes
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_camps_not_shut_down
			has_country_flag = CAN_camps_shut_down
		}
		OR = {
			has_war = no
			surrender_progress < 0.10
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.36.a # Pass the new law
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_work_camps }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_work_camps
				add_idea = CAN_unemployment_insurance_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_work_camps_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_work_camps_2
				add_idea = CAN_unemployment_insurance_idea
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = CAN_unemployment_insurance_idea
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.36.b # Just get rid of the camps
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = CAN_work_camps
				has_idea = CAN_work_camps_2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_work_camps }
			remove_ideas = CAN_work_camps
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_work_camps_2 }
			remove_ideas = CAN_work_camps_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.36.c # We are fine as we are
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.10 }
	}
}

# 1936 Election
country_event = {
	id = canada.50
	title = canada.50.t
	desc = canada.50.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_wlmk_vote

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		CAN_has_elections = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_had_1936_election }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_fallen_government }
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.50"
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas_with_trait = leader_of_the_british_exiles
			multiply_variable = { CAN_conservative_support = 10 }
			multiply_variable = { CAN_liberal_support = 10 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.50.a #Liberals under Mackenzie King
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 34
			modifier = {
				add = CAN_liberal_support
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { king_popularity < 3 }
				check_variable = { king_popularity > 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = { king_popularity < 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_CONSERVATIVE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_LIBERAL_SOCDEM
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = NO_ANIMATED_PORTRAITS
			}
			if = {	
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Edward VIII" ruling_only = yes } }
				set_country_leader_portrait = {
					portrait = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_King_Edward_VIII_Liberal.png"
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {	
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Edward VIII" ruling_only = yes } }
				set_country_leader_portrait = {
					portrait = "GFX_Portrait_Canada_Edward_VII_BOOF_animated"
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable = CAN_conservative_support
		clear_variable = CAN_liberal_support
		set_country_flag = CAN_had_1936_election
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.20 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_soclib_to_coalition = yes
		GBR_returning_king_check = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = CAN_William_Lyon_Mackenzie_King_hog_mli
			if = {
				limit = { CAN_has_exile_govt = yes }
				CAN_add_british_pm_in_exile = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_Louis_St_Laurent_for_sli
			}
			add_ideas = CAN_CD_Howe_eco_mli
			add_ideas = CAN_Ernest_Lapointe_sec_mli
			country_event = { id = canada.51 days = 1 }
			news_event = canada.1140
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.50.b #Conservatives under R.B. Bennett
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 34
			modifier = {
				add = CAN_conservative_support
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { king_popularity > 3 }
				check_variable = { king_popularity < 5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = { king_popularity > 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_LIBERAL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_LIBERAL_SOCDEM
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable = CAN_conservative_support
		clear_variable = CAN_liberal_support
		set_country_flag = CAN_had_1936_election
		set_country_flag = CAN_cons_won_1936
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.20 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_authdem_to_coalition = yes
		GBR_returning_king_check = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = CAN_RB_Bennett_hog_sco
			if = {
				limit = { CAN_has_exile_govt = yes }
				CAN_add_british_pm_in_exile = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_Robert_Manion_for_sco
			}
			add_ideas = CAN_Henry_Herbert_Stevens_eco_sco
			add_ideas = CAN_John_Diefenbaker_sec_sco
			country_event = { id = canada.51 days = 1 }
			news_event = canada.1142
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.50.c #Liberal Coalition with the CCF
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 31
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_CONSERVATIVE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_LIBERAL
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = NO_ANIMATED_PORTRAITS
			}
			if = {	
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Edward VIII" ruling_only = yes } }
				set_country_leader_portrait = {
					portrait = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_King_Edward_VIII_Liberal.png"
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {	
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Edward VIII" ruling_only = yes } }
				set_country_leader_portrait = {
					portrait = "GFX_Portrait_Canada_Edward_VII_BOOF_animated"
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable = CAN_conservative_support
		clear_variable = CAN_liberal_support
		set_country_flag = CAN_had_1936_election
		set_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
		set_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_soclib
		clr_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_marlib
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				current_lib_marlib_pop = party_popularity@market_liberal
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_lib_soclib_pop = party_popularity@social_liberal
			}
			set_popularities = {
				social_liberal = current_lib_marlib_pop
			}
			set_popularities = {
				market_liberal = current_lib_soclib_pop
			}
		}
			
		clear_variable = current_lib_soclib_pop
		clear_variable = current_lib_marlib_pop
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.2 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = -0.10 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.10 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_marlib_to_coalition = yes
		add_socdem_to_coalition = yes
		GBR_returning_king_check = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = CAN_William_Lyon_Mackenzie_King_hog_mli
			if = {
				limit = { CAN_has_exile_govt = yes }
				CAN_add_british_pm_in_exile = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_Thomas_C_Douglas_for_sde
			}
			add_ideas = CAN_CD_Howe_eco_mli
			add_ideas = CAN_J_S_Woodsworth_sec_sde
			country_event = { id = canada.51 days = 1 }
			news_event = canada.1141
		}
	}
}

# Progressives break ranks over Conscription
country_event = {
	id = canada.55
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.55" }
	title = canada.55.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_cabinet2

	desc = {
		text = canada.55.d.limccf
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_C7_limited_cons
			has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.55.d.limnoccf
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_C7_limited_cons
			NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.55.d.fullccf
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_C7_full_cons
			has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.55.d.fullnoccf
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_C7_full_cons
			NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.55.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CAN_C7_limited_cons
				has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
			}
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CAN_C7_limited_cons
				NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition }
			}
			add_political_power = -25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CAN_C7_full_cons
				has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
			}
			add_political_power = -100
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CAN_C7_full_cons
				NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition }
			}
			add_political_power = -75
		}
	}
}

# Voting on the Bill Begins
country_event = {
	id = canada.58
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.58" }
	title = canada.58.t
	desc = canada.58.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_commons1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.58.a #Bill fails
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_LIBERAL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_CONSERVATIVE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_LIBERAL_SOCDEM
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = canada.61 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.58.b #Bill passes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_ABSOLUTE_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_ABSOLUTE_MONARCHY_UK
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_SOCCRED_AUTDEM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_SOCCRED_PATAUT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_NATPOP
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = canada.59 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# Quebec Demonstrations Over Limited Conscription
country_event = {
	id = canada.60
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.60" }
	title = canada.60.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_quebec1

	desc = {
		text = canada.60.d.cons
		trigger = { NOT = { has_liberal_government = yes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.60.d.lib
		trigger = { has_liberal_government = yes }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.60.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = limited_conscription_decision_taken
			}
			add_stability = -0.01
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 466 #Quebec
						state = 468 #Saint Lawrence
						state = 832 #Montreal
					}
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 0.25
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 466 #Quebec
						state = 468 #Saint Lawrence
						state = 832 #Montreal
					}
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Vote of No Confidence - Government Falls
country_event = {
	id = canada.62
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.62" }
	title = canada.62.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_rideau_hall

	desc = {
		text = canada.62.d.cons
		trigger = { has_government = social_conservative }
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.62.d.lib
		trigger = { NOT = { has_government = social_conservative } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		CAN_has_elections = yes
	}

	option = { #Support Bennett
		name = canada.62.a
		trigger = {
			has_liberal_government = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_ABSOLUTE_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_ABSOLUTE_MONARCHY_UK
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_SOCCRED_AUTDEM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_SOCCRED_PATAUT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_NATPOP
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_fallen_government
		custom_effect_tooltip = LOM_elections_three_months
		add_stability = -0.10
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		set_country_flag = CAN_king_support_cons
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = var:current_party_ideology_group
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						election_frequency = 3
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
			GBR_returning_king_check = yes
			country_event = { id = canada.63 days = 10 } #Meighen replaces Bennett
			country_event = { id = canada.65 days = 30 random = 240 } #King Promises New Deal
			country_event = { id = canada.66 days = 50 random = 240 } #Meighen Outlines Bill C-8
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Support King
		name = canada.62.b
		trigger = {
			has_liberal_government = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_ABSOLUTE_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_political_path
						option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_ABSOLUTE_MONARCHY_UK

		trigger = {
			has_liberal_government = yes
		}
	}

		text = canada.622.d_2

			has_liberal_government = no
		}
	}

		name = canada.622.a

		}

		set_country_flag = CAN_king_appointed_govt
		remove_all_ministers = yes

			limit = {
				has_liberal_government = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = CAN_RB_Bennett_hog_sco
				add_ideas = CAN_Robert_Manion_for_sco

			}

		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = CAN_Arthur_Meighen_hog_sco
				add_ideas = CAN_Robert_Manion_for_sco
				if = {

# Meighen Replaces Bennett as Conservative Leader
country_event = {
	id = canada.63
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.63" }
	title = canada.63.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_meighen2

	desc = {
		text = canada.63.d.fallen
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_country_flag = CAN_fallen_government
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.63.d.stepdown
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_fallen_government }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.63.d.challenge
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_conservative }
			has_country_flag = CAN_fallen_government
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.63.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_conservative }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_fallen_government }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		CAN_has_elections = yes
		has_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bennett
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.63.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_conservative }
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = CAN_Arthur_Meighen_hog_sco
		}
		#if = {
		#	limit = { has_idea = CAN_Robert_Manion_for_sco }
		#	remove_ideas = CAN_Robert_Manion_for_sco
		#	add_ideas = CAN_Sidney_Earle_Smith_for_sco
		#}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bennett
		set_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_meighen
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Arthur Meighen"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_Arthur_Meighen.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = moderate_authoritarianism_subtype
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_conservative }
			set_country_leader_ideology = moderate_authoritarianism_subtype
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_soccons_are_modauth
		set_country_flag = CAN_subtype_change
	}
}

# New Election
country_event = {
	id = canada.67
	title = canada.67.t
	desc = canada.67.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		CAN_has_elections = yes
		has_country_flag = CAN_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = CAN_fallen_government
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.67"
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		clr_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas_with_trait = leader_of_the_british_exiles
			multiply_variable = { CAN_conservative_support = 20 }
			multiply_variable = { CAN_liberal_support = 20 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.67.a #Liberals get majority
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = CAN_liberal_support
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { king_popularity < 3 }
				check_variable = { king_popularity > 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = { king_popularity < 2 }
			}
		}
		clear_variable = CAN_conservative_support
		clear_variable = CAN_liberal_support
		clr_country_flag = CAN_fallen_government
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.20 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_soclib_to_coalition = yes
		GBR_returning_king_check = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = CAN_William_Lyon_Mackenzie_King_hog_mli
			if = {
				limit = { CAN_has_exile_govt = yes }
				CAN_add_british_pm_in_exile = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_Vincent_Massey_for_mli
			}
			add_ideas = CAN_CD_Howe_eco_mli
			add_ideas = CAN_Ernest_Lapointe_sec_mli
			country_event = { id = canada.68 days = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.67.b #Conservatives get majority
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = CAN_conservative_support
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { king_popularity > 3 }
				check_variable = { king_popularity < 5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = { king_popularity > 4 }
			}
		}
		clear_variable = CAN_conservative_support
		clear_variable = CAN_liberal_support
		clr_country_flag = CAN_fallen_government
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.20 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_soccreds_exist }
			}
			add_authdem_to_coalition = yes
		}
		GBR_returning_king_check = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_meighen }
				add_ideas = CAN_Arthur_Meighen_hog_sco
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_manion }
				add_ideas = CAN_Robert_Manion_hog_sco
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_RB_Bennett_hog_sco
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CAN_has_exile_govt = yes }
				CAN_add_british_pm_in_exile = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_Sidney_Earle_Smith_for_sco
			}
			add_ideas = CAN_Stephen_Leacock_eco_sco
			add_ideas = CAN_John_Diefenbaker_sec_sco
			country_event = { id = canada.69 days = 10 }
		}
	}
}

		add_ideas = CAN_mounties_1
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas_with_trait = security_minister }
		add_ideas = CAN_Maxwell_Knight_sec_pau

		set_country_flag = CAN_C7_passed
		clear_variable = chance_pass
		clear_variable = vote
		clr_country_flag = CAN_C7_full_cons
		clr_country_flag = CAN_C7_limited_cons
		clr_country_flag = CAN_C7_no_cons
		clr_country_flag = CAN_C7_econ_lib
		clr_country_flag = CAN_C7_econ_conserv
		clr_country_flag = CAN_C7_econ_comp
		clr_country_flag = CAN_C7_sec_knight
		clr_country_flag = CAN_C7_sec_lapointe

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { 
				id = canada.100 
				days = 3 
				random_days = 5
			}
			set_country_flag = CAN_C7_full_cons_complete
		}
	}
}

# Mackenzie King Retires
country_event = {
	id = canada.70
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.70" }
	title = canada.70.t
	desc = canada.70.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_mackenzie_king

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_lib_leader_stlaurent }
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.70.a
		clr_country_flag = CAN_lib_leader_king
		set_country_flag = CAN_lib_leader_stlaurent
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_marlib 
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_liberal
				election_frequency = 60
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_marlib_to_coalition = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = CAN_Louis_St_Laurent_hog_sli
				set_country_leader_ideology = national_liberalism_subtype
				set_country_flag = CAN_soclibs_are_natlib
				set_country_flag = CAN_subtype_change 
				if = { 
					limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soclibs_are_agrarian } 
					clr_country_flag = CAN_soclibs_are_agrarian 
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soclibs_are_spiritualist } 
					clr_country_flag = CAN_soclibs_are_spiritualist 
				}
				if = {
					limit = { CAN_has_exile_govt = yes }
					CAN_add_british_pm_in_exile = yes
				}
				else = {
					add_ideas = CAN_Mitchell_Hepburn_for_sli
				}
				add_ideas = CAN_Alphonse_Fournier_eco_sli
				add_ideas = CAN_Stuart_Garson_sec_sli
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			hidden_effect = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Louis St. Laurent"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_Louis_St_Laurent.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = national_liberalism_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Charles Gavan Power"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_Charles_Gavan_Power.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = marlib_national_liberalism_subtype
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_marlib
		set_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_soclib
	}
}

# Mackenzie King Ideology Picker
country_event = {
	id = canada.700
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.700" }
	title = canada.700.t
	desc = {
		text = canada.700.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.700.d_ccf
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_mackenzie_king3

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_idea = CAN_William_Lyon_Mackenzie_King_hog_mli
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.700.a
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_marlib 
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_liberal
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_marlib_to_coalition = yes

			clr_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_marlib
			set_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_soclib
			set_variable = {
				current_lib_marlib_pop = party_popularity@market_liberal
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_lib_soclib_pop = party_popularity@social_liberal
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_lib_marlib_pop
				value = current_lib_soclib_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = current_lib_marlib_pop
			}
			set_popularities = {
				market_liberal = current_lib_soclib_pop
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.700.b
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_marlib 
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_liberal
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_marlib_to_coalition = yes
		
			clr_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_marlib
			set_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_soclib
			set_variable = {
				current_lib_marlib_pop = party_popularity@market_liberal
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_lib_soclib_pop = party_popularity@social_liberal
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_lib_marlib_pop
				value = current_lib_soclib_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = current_lib_marlib_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = -0.1
			}
	
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = soclib_agrarianism_subtype
		set_country_flag = CAN_soclibs_are_agrarian
		set_country_flag = CAN_subtype_change 
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.700.c
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_soclib
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = market_liberal
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_soclib_to_coalition = yes
		
			clr_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_soclib
			set_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_marlib
			set_variable = {
				current_lib_soclib_pop = party_popularity@social_liberal
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_lib_marlib_pop = party_popularity@market_liberal
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_lib_soclib_pop
				value = current_lib_marlib_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = current_lib_soclib_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = -0.1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
	}
	
	
	
	option = {
		name = canada.700.e
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_marlib 
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_liberal
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_marlib_to_coalition = yes
		
			clr_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_marlib
			set_country_flag = CAN_libs_are_soclib
			set_variable = {
				current_lib_marlib_pop = party_popularity@market_liberal
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_lib_soclib_pop = party_popularity@social_liberal
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_lib_marlib_pop
				value = current_lib_soclib_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = current_lib_marlib_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = -0.1
			}
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = soclib_spiritualism_subtype
		set_country_flag = CAN_soclibs_are_spiritualist
		set_country_flag = CAN_subtype_change 
	}
}

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Major James Coldwell"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_Major_James_Coldwell.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		if = { 
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_J_S_Woodsworth_sec_sde }
			remove_ideas_with_trait = security_minister
			add_ideas = CAN_Hazen_Argue_sec_sde
		}
	    }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.72.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.04
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_2 = yes
		set_country_flag = CAN_ccf_leader_woodsworth
	}
}

# J.S. Woodsworth dies
country_event = {
	id = canada.720
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.720" }
	title = canada.720.t
	desc = {
		text = canada.720.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_ccf_leader_woodsworth }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.720.d_ccf_leader
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_ccf_leader_woodsworth
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_woodsworth

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.720.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_ccf_leader_woodsworth }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.02
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.720.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_ccf_leader_woodsworth
		}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_ccf_leader_woodsworth
		set_country_flag = CAN_ccf_leader_coldwell
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_JS_Woodsworth_hog_sde }
			remove_ideas = CAN_JS_Woodsworth_hog_sde
			add_ideas = CAN_Major_James_Coldwell_hog_sde
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Major James Coldwell"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_Major_James_Coldwell.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_J_S_Woodsworth_sec_sde }
			remove_ideas_with_trait = security_minister
			add_ideas = CAN_Hazen_Argue_sec_sde
		}
	}
}

			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_douglas }
				add_ideas = CAN_CH_Douglas_hog_ade
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_hargrave }
				add_ideas = CAN_John_Hargrave_hog_pau
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_bennett }
				add_ideas = CAN_W_A_C_Bennett_hog_ade
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_aberhart }
				add_ideas = CAN_William_Aberhart_hog_pau
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_haldeman }
				add_ideas = CAN_Joshua_N_Haldeman_hog_pau
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_herridge }
				add_ideas = CAN_William_Duncan_Herridge_hog_ade
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_Ernest_Manning_hog_ade
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CAN_has_exile_govt = yes }
				CAN_add_british_pm_in_exile = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { CAN_has_exile_govt = yes } 
					has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_herridge
				}
				add_ideas = CAN_Chester_Reynolds_for_ade
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_William_Duncan_Herridge_for_ade
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_bennett }
				add_ideas = CAN_Victor_Quelch_eco_ade
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_WAC_Bennett_eco_ade
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_low }
				add_ideas = CAN_Ernest_Manning_sec_ade
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_Solon_Earl_Low_sec_ade
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					date > 1941.1.1
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bracken }
				}
				country_event = { id = canada.76 days = 60 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bracken
				}
				country_event = { id = canada.760 days = 60 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_drew
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_Drew_was_PM }
				}
				country_event = { id = canada.7601 days = 60 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_lib_leader_stlaurent
				}
				country_event = { id = canada.761 days = 60 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_ccf_leader_coldwell
				}
				country_event = { id = canada.762 days = 60 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_ccf_leader_argue
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CAN_CCF_victory
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = canada.7621 days = 60 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Conservative party rebranded under Bracken
country_event = {
	id = canada.76
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.76" }
	title = canada.76.t
	desc = canada.76.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_bracken

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.76.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			long_name = CAN_prog_conservative_party_long
			name = CAN_prog_conservative_party
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bracken
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_conservative }
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = CAN_John_Bracken_hog_sco
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_John_Bracken_eco_sco }
			remove_ideas = CAN_John_Bracken_eco_sco
			add_ideas = CAN_Stephen_Leacock_eco_sco
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "John Bracken"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_John_Bracken.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = toryism_subtype
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bennett
		clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_stevens
		clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_manion
		clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_meighen
	}
}

# Diefenbaker suceeds Bracken
country_event = {
	id = canada.760
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.760" }
	title = canada.760.t
	desc = {
		text = canada.760.d_con_PM
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_Bracken_was_PM
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.760.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = CAN_Bracken_was_PM
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_conservative_leadership

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_manning
		}
	}

	option = { #Dief will be the Chief again! (and not as a natpop for some asinine reason)
		name = canada.760.a
		
		clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bracken
		set_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_diefenbaker
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_government = social_conservative 
				has_idea = CAN_John_Bracken_hog_sco
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = CAN_John_Diefenbaker_hog_sco
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_John_Diefenbaker_sec_sco }
			remove_ideas = CAN_John_Diefenbaker_sec_sco
			add_ideas = CAN_Gordon_Graydon_sec_sco
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "John Diefenbaker"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_John_Diefenbaker.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = progressive_conservatism_subtype
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.02
		}
	}
	
	option = { #George Drew (also a Natpop in KR for some insane reason)
		name = canada.760.b
		
		clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bracken
		set_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_drew
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_government = social_conservative 
				has_idea = CAN_John_Bracken_hog_sco
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = CAN_George_A_Drew_hog_sco
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "George A. Drew"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_George_A_Drew.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = progressive_conservatism_subtype
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.02
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Keep Bracken
		name = canada.760.c
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.02
		}
	}
}

			limit = { has_idea = CAN_Real_Caouette_sec_pau }
			remove_ideas = CAN_Real_Caouette_sec_pau
			add_ideas = CAN_WAC_Bennett_sec_ade
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Réal Caouette"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/QUE/Portrait_Quebec_Real_Caouette.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_social_credit_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Bennett
		name = canada.764.c
		clr_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_blackmore
		set_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_bennett
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				has_idea = CAN_JH_Blackmore_hog_ade
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = CAN_W_A_C_Bennett_hog_ade
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_WAC_Bennett_eco_ade }
			remove_ideas = CAN_WAC_Bennett_eco_ade
			add_ideas = CAN_Victor_Quelch_eco_ade
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_WAC_Bennett_sec_ade }
			remove_ideas = CAN_WAC_Bennett_sec_ade
			add_ideas = CAN_Solon_Earl_Low_sec_ade
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "W.A.C. Bennett"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_W_A_C_Bennett.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_social_credit_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Haldeman
		name = canada.763.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_technocracy_inc
		}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_herridge
		set_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_haldeman
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				has_idea = CAN_JH_Blackmore_hog_ade
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = CAN_Joshua_N_Haldeman_hog_pau
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Joshua N. Haldeman"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_Joshua_N_Haldeman.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_social_credit_subtype
			}
		}
	}
}

# King replaces British PM
country_event = {
	id = canada.77
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.77" }
	title = canada.77.t
	desc = canada.77.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_rideau

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		OR = {
			has_idea = CAN_Henry_Page_Croft_lobe_pau
			has_idea = CAN_Robert_Cecil_lobe_ade
			has_idea = CAN_Edward_Halifax_lobe_sco
			has_idea = CAN_Stanley_Baldwin_lobe_ade
			has_idea = CAN_Anthony_Eden_lobe_ade
			has_idea = CAN_Neville_Chamberlain_lobe_ade
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = CAN_rally_the_country }
		has_country_flag = KR_british_king_base
		has_country_flag = CAN_king_replaces_pm
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.77.a
		clr_country_flag = CAN_king_replaces_pm
		GBR_reset_GB_PM = yes
		add_ideas = CAN_Robert_Vansittart_lobe_ade
		GBR = { set_country_flag = GBR_Vansittart_PM }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_exile_influence_decrease
		CAN_improve_canadian_influence_bop = yes
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { king_influence > 0 } }
			subtract_from_variable = { king_influence = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { king_influence = 0 }
		}
	}
}


### QUEBEC EVENTS

# Riots Across Quebec (response to full conscription)
country_event = {
	id = canada.100
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.100" }
	title = canada.100.t
	desc = canada.100.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_conscription_protest_quebec

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		is_subject = no
		OR = {
			466 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN } #Quebec
			468 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN } #Saint Lawrence
			832 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN } #Montreal
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = extensive_conscription
			has_idea = service_by_requirement
			has_idea = all_adults_serve
			has_idea = scraping_the_barrel
		}
		NOT = {
			surrender_progress > 0
			has_war_with = USA
			has_war_with = CSA
			has_war_with = CAL
			has_war_with = TEX
			has_war_with = NEE
			has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_was_in_flames
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.100.a
		set_country_flag = CAN_quebec_was_in_flames
		add_stability = -0.10
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_2
				add_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_3
				add_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_1
					has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_2
					has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_3
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_1
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = CAN
				OR = {
					state = 466 #Quebec
					state = 468 #Saint Lawrence
					state = 832 #Montreal
				}
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_3 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = canada.101 days = 15 random = 720 } #Bounce event
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = { id = canada.112 days = 1 }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = canada.451
				days = 65
				random_days = 33
			}
		}
		add_ideas = CAN_quebec_in_flames_idea
	}
}

# Hidden bounce event for resistance events
country_event = {
	id = canada.101
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.101" }

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_idea = CAN_quebec_in_flames_idea
	}

	option = {
		name = AI_OPTION #Industrial Sabotage
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_3 }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_2 }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_1 }
				}
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_quebec_civ
		country_event = canada.102
	}
	option = {
		name = AI_OPTION #Arms Sabotage
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_3 }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_2 }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_1 }
				}
				arms_factory > 0
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_quebec_arms
		country_event = canada.102
	}
	option = {
		name = AI_OPTION #Riots
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_3 }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_2 }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_1 }
				}
				infrastructure > 2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_quebec_riots
		country_event = canada.102
	}
	option = {
		name = AI_OPTION #Ringleaders Arrested
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_3 }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_2 }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_quebec_ringleader
		country_event = canada.102
	}
	option = {
		name = AI_OPTION #Nothing
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				NOT = {
					any_owned_state = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_3 }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				NOT = {
					any_owned_state = {
						OR = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_3 }
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_2 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = canada.101 days = 90 random = 1080 } #Bounce event
	}
}

# Resistance event
country_event = {
	id = canada.102
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_bombing

	title = {
		text = canada.102.t.civ
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_civ }
	}
	title = {
		text = canada.102.t.arms
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_arms }
	}
	title = {
		text = canada.102.t.riots
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_riots }
	}
	title = {
		text = canada.102.t.ringleader
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_ringleader }
	}

	desc = {
		text = canada.102.d.civ
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_civ }
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.102.d.arms
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_arms }
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.102.d.riots
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_riots }
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.102.d.ringleader
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_ringleader }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.102"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_civ }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_3 }
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_2 }
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_1 }
						}
						industrial_complex > 0
					}
					save_event_target_as = french_state
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_arms }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_3 }
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_2 }
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_1 }
						}
						arms_factory > 0
					}
					save_event_target_as = french_state
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_riots }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_3 }
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_2 }
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_1 }
						}
						infrastructure > 2
					}
					save_event_target_as = french_state
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_ringleader }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_3 }
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_french_resistance_2 }
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = french_state
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.102.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_ringleader } }
		event_target:french_state = {
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_civ } }
				damage_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					damage = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_arms } }
				damage_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					damage = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_riots } }
				damage_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					damage = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_quebec_civ
		clr_country_flag = CAN_quebec_arms
		clr_country_flag = CAN_quebec_riots
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = canada.101 days = 90 random = 1080 } #Bounce event
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.102.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_ringleader }
		event_target:french_state = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_resistance_effects_reduced
			CAN_reduce_french_resistance = yes
		}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_quebec_ringleader
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = canada.101 days = 90 random = 1080 } #Bounce event
		}
	}
}

# The War Measures Act (fired by focus)
country_event = {
	id = canada.108
	title = canada.108.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_wma_invoked

	desc = {
		text = canada.108.d.war
		trigger = {
			has_war = yes
			any_enemy_country = { is_actual_major = yes }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.108.d.nowar
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war = no
				NOT = { any_enemy_country = { is_actual_major = yes } }
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.108"
		remove_all_ministers = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.108.a
		set_country_flag = CAN_warmeasact_invoked
		add_political_power = 100
		add_war_support = -0.10
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_suppress_quebec
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_suppress_stlawrence
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_suppress_montreal
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_emergency_draft
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = extensive_conscription
					has_idea = service_by_requirement
					has_idea = all_adults_serve
					has_idea = scraping_the_barrel
				}
			}
			unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_expand_conscription_policies
		}
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_expand_secret_police
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { king_influence < 5 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_exile_influence_increase
			add_to_variable = { king_influence = 1 }
			CAN_calc_exile_influence_effects = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { king_popularity > 0 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_king_popularity_decrease
			subtract_from_variable = { king_popularity = 1 }
			CAN_calc_royal_visit_effects = yes
		}
		CAN_improve_exile_influence_big_bop = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = {
				CAN_Arthur_Meighen_hog_sco
				CAN_Andrew_Carnell_eco_ade
				CAN_WAC_Bennett_sec_ade
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = { id = canada.113 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = canada.111.t
	desc = canada.111.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_meighen

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.111"
		remove_all_ministers = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.111.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_king_popularity_decrease
		set_variable = { king_popularity = 1 }
		CAN_calc_royal_visit_effects = yes
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = 200
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = -0.20 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.20 }
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_consolidate_power
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_expand_labour_camps
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_increase_factory_prod
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CAN_fund_the_military
		set_country_flag = CAN_WMA_absolutism
		set_country_flag = CAN_royal_perogative
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister
			remove_ideas_with_trait = security_minister
			add_ideas = {
				CAN_Lord_Mountbatten_eco_pau
				CAN_Maxwell_Knight_sec_pau
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = { id = canada.114 days = 1 }
			}
			country_event = { id = canada.116 days = 7 }
		}
	}
}

# News: Conscription Crisis in Quebec
news_event = {
	id = canada.112
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.112" }
	title = canada.112.t
	desc = canada.112.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_CAN_conscription

	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	show_major = {
		NOT = { tag = CAN }
		OR = {
			regional_north_america_news = yes
			regional_europe_news = yes
			is_in_faction_with = CAN
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.112.a
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = CAN
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.112.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
			}
		}
	}
}

# French tensions lessen
country_event = {
	id = canada.115
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.115" }
	title = canada.115.t
	desc = canada.115.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_montreal

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		OR = {
			has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_1
			has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_2
			has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_3
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = volunteer_only
			has_idea = limited_conscription
		}
		has_country_flag = CAN_C7_passed
		CAN_has_elections = yes
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_war = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_idea = limited_conscription
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_3
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.115.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_1 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_1
				add_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_2
				add_idea = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_3
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_ideas = CAN_anglo_french_tensions_3
		}
	}
}

	id = canada.117
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.117" }
	title = canada.117.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_quebec1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	desc = {
		text = canada.117.d.notfra
		trigger = { NOT = { has_war_with = FRA } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.117.d.fra
		trigger = { has_war_with = FRA }
	}

	trigger = {
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.117.a
		add_stability = -0.025
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 466 #Quebec
					state = 468 #Saint Lawrence
					state = 832 #Montreal
				}
			}
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.5
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = canada.150
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.150" }
	title = canada.150.t
	desc = canada.150.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_parliament1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.150.a #Offer them aid for an alliance
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = ENG_CANIRE_support }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 65
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					has_war_with = ENG
					has_war_with = GER
				}
			}
		}
		IRE = {
			country_event = { id = canada.151 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.150.b #Offer them protection for bases
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				IRE = { gives_military_access_to = CAN }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_global_flag = ENG_CANIRE_protection
			}
		}
		IRE = {
			country_event = { id = canada.158 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

# Ireland offered alliance for aid
country_event = {
	id = canada.151
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.151" }
	title = canada.151.t
	desc = canada.151.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_parliament1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
		is_in_faction = no
		has_socialist_government = no
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.151.a #We want a guarantee of full independence
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = ENT_britain_agree_northire }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = canada.152
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.151.b #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_global_flag = ENT_britain_agree_northire
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = canada.155
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = KR_approves_of_govt }
			effect_tooltip = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.151.c #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				CAN = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = ENG
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = canada.156
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt }
		}
	}
}

			factor = 70
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_to_faction = IRE
		IRE = {
			country_event = canada.153
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = canada.157 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CAN_promised_ireland_ind
			GBR = { set_country_flag = CAN_promised_ireland_ind }
			every_state = {
				limit = { region = 4 } #Ireland
				clear_variable = ambition_area_@GBR
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.152.b #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		IRE = { country_event = canada.154 }
	}
}

# How does Ireland want to use the aid?
country_event = {
	id = canada.157
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.157" }
	title = canada.157.t
	desc = canada.157.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_parliament1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_in_faction_with = CAN
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.157.a #Civilian
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = CAN_imp_investment_1
			days = 180
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = IRE
				is_core_of = IRE
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.157.b #Military
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = CAN_imp_advisors_1
			days = 180
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = IRE
				is_core_of = IRE
				arms_factory > 0
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.157.c #Naval
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = CAN_iedc_naval1
			days = 180
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = IRE
				is_core_of = IRE
				dockyard > 0
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = dockyard
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = canada.158
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.158" }
	title = canada.158.t
	desc = canada.158.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_parliament1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
		is_in_faction = no
		has_socialist_government = no
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.158.a #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_has_treaty_with_IRE
		add_political_power = 50
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = KR_approves_of_govt }
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { NOT = { is_guaranteed_by = CAN } }
					}
					give_guarantee = ROOT
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = military_access
					active = yes
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = docking_rights
					active = yes
				}
			}
			country_event = canada.159
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.158.b #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { has_global_flag = ENG_CANIRE_protection }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt }
			country_event = canada.160
		}
	}
}

			factor = 75

			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = ICE_danish_bailout }
			}

			}
		}
		ICE_improve_economy_2 = yes
		complete_national_focus = ICE_Ottawa_King
		FROM = {
			country_event = canada.171
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = KR_approves_of_govt }
			effect_tooltip = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.170.b #Refuse

			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_idea = ICE_danish_bailout
			}
		}
	}
}
