# the King thinks it's time to attack
country_event = {
	id = canada.174
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.174" }
	title = canada.174.t
	desc = canada.174.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_army2

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		has_country_flag = KR_british_king_base
		is_subject = no
		can_declare_war_on = ENG
		date > 1939.1.1
		OR = {
			ENG = { has_war_with = GER }
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_tech = transport
					has_tech = mtg_transport
				}
				has_completed_focus = CAN_project_plough
				has_completed_focus = CAN_economic_recovery
				has_completed_focus = CAN_deal_with_admiralty
				has_completed_focus = CAN_new_munitions_plants
			}
			AND = {
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
				has_completed_focus = CAN_project_plough
				has_completed_focus = CAN_economic_recovery
				has_completed_focus = CAN_deal_with_admiralty
			}
		}
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.174.a #Perhaps he's right...
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_authoritarian_government = no
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = CAN_contact_loyalists
						has_completed_focus = CAN_economic_recovery
						has_completed_focus = CAN_deal_with_admiralty
						has_completed_focus = CAN_new_munitions_plants
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_authoritarian_government = no
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ENG
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.174.b #We will attack when we're ready, no sooner
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

# Contacting the British Loyalists (fired by decision)
country_event = {
	id = canada.175
	title = canada.175.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_homecoming

	desc = {
		text = canada.175.d.scotland
		trigger = {
			ENG = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_state = {
						OR = {
							region = 1
							region = 2
						}
						is_core_of = ENG
						is_controlled_by = CAN
					}
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					region = 3
					is_core_of = ENG
					NOT = { state = 938 } #Northern Isles
					is_controlled_by = CAN
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.175.d.england
		trigger = {
			ENG = {
				any_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						region = 1
						region = 2
					}
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_controlled_by = CAN
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.175"
		hidden_effect = {
			ENG = {
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 1
							region = 2
							region = 3
						}
						is_core_of = ENG
						NOT = { state = 938 } #Northern Isles
						is_controlled_by = CAN
					}
					save_event_target_as = invasion_state
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.175.a
		set_country_flag = CAN_has_british_loyalists
		if = {
			limit = {
				ENG = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								region = 1
								region = 2
							}
							is_core_of = ENG
							is_controlled_by = CAN
						}
					}
					any_owned_state = {
						region = 3
						is_core_of = ENG
						NOT = { state = 938 } #Northern Isles
						is_controlled_by = CAN
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_loyalists_spawn_sct
			hidden_effect = { load_oob = "CAN_loyalist_sct" }
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_loyalists_spawn_eng
			hidden_effect = { load_oob = "CAN_loyalist_eng" }
		}
		event_target:invasion_state = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"6th Loyalist Volunteers\" division_template = \"Loyalist Rebels\"  start_experience_factor = 0.1"
				owner = ROOT
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"3rd Loyalist Elite Division\" division_template = \"Loyalist Mountaineers\"  start_experience_factor = 0.0"
				owner = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ENG = { country_event = canada.176 }
		}
	}
}

				transfer_state = 119

					add_manpower = 80000
					load_oob = "IRE_REV_FULL_SUPP"
					add_political_power = 100
					add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.35 }
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = 2500 producer = CAN }
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Gearóid Ó Cuinneagáin"
						desc = "POLITICS_GEAROID_O_CUINNEAGAIN_DESC"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/IRE/Portrait_Ireland_Gearoid_O_Cuinneagain.png"
						expire = "1.1.1"
						ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}

			add_manpower = 80000

# French resistance collapses
country_event = {
	id = canada.179
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.179" }
	title = canada.179.t
	desc = canada.179.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_army1

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		has_capitulated = yes
		is_government_in_exile = yes
		NOT = { has_legitimacy > 20 }
		CAN = { is_faction_leader = yes }
		126 = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = CAN
					is_in_faction_with = CAN
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.179"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					FRA = {
						is_in_faction_with = ENG
						has_capitulated = no
					}
				}
				FRA = { set_faction_leader = yes }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					SOV = {
						is_in_faction_with = ENG
						has_capitulated = no
					}
				}
				SOV = { set_faction_leader = yes }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					any_country = {
						is_actual_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = ENG
						has_capitulated = no
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						is_actual_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = ENG
						has_capitulated = no
					}
					set_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.179.a
		if = {
			limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		else = {
			leave_faction = yes
		}
	}
}

		text = canada.200.d.assass
		trigger = { USA = { has_country_flag = USA_assassinated_reed } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.200.d.peace
		trigger = { USA = { has_country_flag = USA_ACW_compromise_rejected } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.200.d
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = USA_ACW_compromise_rejected
					has_country_flag = USA_assassinated_reed
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.200.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { refugee_states = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = CAN_king_edward_VIII
				}
				country_event = { id = entente.63 days = 30 random = 10 } # Edward Meets with Refugees
			}
			country_event = { id = canada.206 days = 60 random = 480 } # American trade impacted
			country_event = { id = canada.207 days = 90 random = 720 } # Clashes in Windsor
			country_event = { id = canada.210 days = 150 random = 720 } # Sympathy Strike for the CSA/AUS
		}
	}
}

# American refugees flood into state (repeating event)
country_event = {
	id = canada.202
	title = canada.202.t
	desc = canada.202.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_refugees

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		is_subject = no
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		check_variable = { refugee_states < 10 }
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = USA
			has_war_with = CSA
			has_war_with = CAL
			has_war_with = TEX
			has_war_with = NEE
			has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sec
			has_country_flag = CAN_ref_shipped_to_nee
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			is_controlled_by = CAN
			NOT = {
				has_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_1
				has_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_2
			}
			any_neighbor_state = {
				check_variable = { state_population > 750000 }
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = CSA
					controller = {
						is_american_tag = yes
						NOT = { owns_state = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			check_variable = { refugee_states < 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			check_variable = { refugee_states > 2 }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.202"
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = CAN
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_1
						has_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_2
					}
					any_neighbor_state = {
						check_variable = { state_population > 750000 }
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = CSA
							controller = {
								is_american_tag = yes
								NOT = { owns_state = PREV }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = refugee_state
				random_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state_population > 750000 }
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = CSA
							controller = {
								is_american_tag = yes
								NOT = { owns_state = PREV }
							}
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = flee_from_state
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.202.a
		event_target:refugee_state = {
			set_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_1
			add_state_modifier = {
				modifier = {
					local_supplies = -0.20
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_help }
			add_manpower = 7500
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sam }
			add_manpower = 12500
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { refugee_states = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# Even more American refugees flood into state (repeating event)
country_event = {
	id = canada.203
	title = canada.203.t
	desc = canada.203.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_refugees2

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		is_subject = no
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
		check_variable = { refugee_states < 10 }
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = USA
			has_war_with = CSA
			has_war_with = CAL
			has_war_with = TEX
			has_war_with = NEE
			has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sec
			has_country_flag = CAN_ref_shipped_to_nee
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			is_controlled_by = CAN
			has_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_1
			any_neighbor_state = {
				check_variable = { state_population > 1250000 }
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = CSA
					controller = {
						is_american_tag = yes
						NOT = { owns_state = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			check_variable = { refugee_states > 2 }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.203"
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = CAN
					has_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_1
					any_neighbor_state = {
						check_variable = { state_population > 1250000 }
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = CSA
							controller = {
								is_american_tag = yes
								NOT = { owns_state = PREV }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = refugee_state
				random_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state_population > 1250000 }
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = CSA
							controller = {
								is_american_tag = yes
								NOT = { owns_state = PREV }
							}
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = flee_from_state
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.203.a
		event_target:refugee_state = {
			clr_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_1
			set_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_2
			add_state_modifier = {
				modifier = {
					local_supplies = -0.20
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_help }
			add_manpower = 7500
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sam }
			add_manpower = 12500
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { refugee_states = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# New Home of the Free (fired by focus)
country_event = {
	id = canada.211
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.211" }
	title = canada.211.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_parliament1

	desc = {
		text = canada.211.d.nee
		trigger = {
			NEE = { is_subject_of = CAN }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.211.d.nonee
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				NEE = { is_subject_of = CAN }
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.211.a # Security is paramount
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				NEE = { is_subject_of = CAN }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_liberal_government = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_1 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_1
				add_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sec
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_2
				add_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sec
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.211.b # Ship them to New England
		trigger = {
			NEE = { is_subject_of = CAN }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_liberal_government = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_ref_shipped_to_nee
		add_political_power = -50
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_1 }
			remove_ideas = CAN_refugee_crisis_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_2 }
			remove_ideas = CAN_refugee_crisis_2
		}
		NEE = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt }
			country_event = canada.212
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.211.c # We need to help them, within reason
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_1 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_1
				add_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_help
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_2
				add_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_help
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.211.e # enact Project Samaritan
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_political_power < 0
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -250
		add_stability = -0.10
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_1 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_1
				add_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sam
			}
		}

				remove_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_2
				add_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sam
			}
		}
	}

# American refugees leave for home once ACW is over
country_event = {
	id = canada.214
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.214" }
	title = canada.214.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_refugees2

	desc = {
		text = canada.214.d.ceasefirecsa
		trigger = {
			country_exists = CSA
			has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.214.d.ceasefirenocsa
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = CSA }
			has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.214.d.noceasefirecsa
		trigger = {
			country_exists = CSA
			NOT = { has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.214.d.noceasefirenocsa
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = CSA }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		OR = {
			has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_1
			has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_2
			has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sec
			has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_help
			has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sam
			check_variable = { refugee_states > 0 }
		}
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.214.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = CAN_american_recruitment
				OR = {
					has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_help
					has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sam
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { american_recruit = refugee_states }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_help }
				multiply_temp_variable = { american_recruit = -7500 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sam }
				multiply_temp_variable = { american_recruit = -12500 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = CSA
					has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = { american_recruit = 0.40 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = CSA
					NOT = { has_global_flag = PSA_rockies_ceasefire }
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = { american_recruit = 0.20 }
			}
			else = {
				multiply_temp_variable = { american_recruit = 0.60 }
			}
			add_manpower = american_recruit
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_1 }
			remove_ideas = CAN_refugee_crisis_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_2 }
			remove_ideas = CAN_refugee_crisis_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sec }
			remove_ideas = CAN_refugee_crisis_sec
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_help }
			remove_ideas = CAN_refugee_crisis_help
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_sam }
			remove_ideas = CAN_refugee_crisis_sam
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_variable = refugee_states
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_1 }
				clr_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_1
				add_state_modifier = {
					modifier = {
						local_supplies = 0.20
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_2 }
				clr_state_flag = CAN_american_refugee_2
				add_state_modifier = {
					modifier = {
						local_supplies = 0.40
					}
				}
			}
			NEE = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = CAN_refugee_crisis_2 }
					remove_ideas = CAN_refugee_crisis_2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.216" }

	desc = canada.216.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_prime_minister_new_england

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.216.a #We value their alliance
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_country_flag = CAN_returned_land
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				CAN = {
					any_owned_state = {
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				OR = {
					is_claimed_by = CAN
					is_core_of = CAN
				}
			}
			CAN = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		CAN = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = KR_close_allies }
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						NOT = {
							is_claimed_by = CAN
							is_core_of = CAN
						}
					}
					ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						ROOT = { is_in_faction = no }
					}
					add_to_faction = ROOT
				}
			}
			country_event = canada.217
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.216.b #We are fine as we are
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = NEE_refused_home_rule
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt }
			country_event = canada.218
		}
	}
}

				FROM = { tag = TEX }
			}
			add_ideas = ACW_support_aus
		}

		}
	}
}

		name = canada.220.a
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = CAN }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = ACW_entente_helping }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { tag = CAN } }
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = canada.219
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_north_america = yes
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
						tag = CAN
						is_in_faction_with = CAN
					}
				}
				country_event = canada.221
			}
		}
	}
}

					tag = CAN

				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT 	modifier = KR_approves_of_govt }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT 	modifier = KR_approves_of_govt }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}

				relation = docking_rights
				active = yes
			}
			ROOT = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = PREV
					relation = docking_rights
					active = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				news_event = canada.230
			}
		}
	}
}

# CSA becomes aware of possible intervention
country_event = {
	id = canada.223
	title = canada.223.t
	desc = canada.223.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_defense_scheme_no_1

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		is_subject = no
		CAN = {
			is_subject = no
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = USA
				has_war_with = CAL
				has_war_with = TEX
				has_war_with = NEE
				has_war_with = CSA
			}
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = CAN_crossing_the_border
				focus_progress = {
					focus = CAN_crossing_the_border
					progress > 0.25
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.223"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { CAN_strike_cost = 50 }
			CAN = {
				set_variable = { CSA_strikes = 0 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.223.a
		set_country_flag = CSA_can_delay_canada
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CSA_delay_canadian_intervention
	}
}

# Asking surviving ACW country to join Entente
country_event = {
	id = canada.227
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.227" }
	title = canada.227.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_american_canadian_soldiers

	desc = {
		text = canada.227.d
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_state = {
						OR = {
							is_mainland_america = yes
							state = 463 #Alaska
							state = 629 #Hawaii
							state = 685 #Panama Canal
							state = 686 #Puerto Rica
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.227.d.owned
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				any_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						is_mainland_america = yes
						state = 463 #Alaska
						state = 629 #Hawaii
						state = 685 #Panama Canal
						state = 686 #Puerto Rica
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.227.a #Yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_country_flag = USA_compromise_reached
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = COR_foreign_policy
						option = COR_FOREIGN_POLICY_REICHSPAKT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = COR_foreign_policy
						option = COR_FOREIGN_POLICY_EXPANSIONISM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = COR_foreign_policy
						option = COR_FOREIGN_POLICY_ISOLATIONISM
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = CAN
					NOT = { is_core_of = CAN }
					OR = {
						is_mainland_america = yes
						state = 463 #Alaska
						state = 629 #Hawaii
						state = 685 #Panama Canal
						state = 686 #Puerto Rica
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
					remove_claim_by = CAN
				}
				ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			effect_tooltip = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
			country_event = canada.228
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.227.b #No
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CAN = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_supports_@ROOT }
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = CAN_supports_USA
						has_country_flag = CAN_supports_CAL
						has_country_flag = CAN_supports_TEX
						has_country_flag = CAN_supports_COR
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CAN = { has_country_flag = CAN_supports_@ROOT }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_returned_land }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CAN = { NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_supports_@ROOT } }
				has_country_flag = CAN_returned_land
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			country_event = canada.229
		}
	}
}

# UK has been restored
country_event = {
	id = canada.300
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.300" }
	title = canada.300.t
	desc = canada.300.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_fleeing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.300.a
		add_war_support = -0.20
		add_ideas = CAN_british_exodus
		remove_ideas_with_trait = leader_of_the_british_exiles
		set_country_flag = Archibald_Montgomery_Massingberd_dead
		set_country_flag = Sir_Edmund_Ironside_dead
		set_country_flag = JFC_Fuller_dead
		set_country_flag = Claude_Auchinleck_dead
		set_country_flag = Harold_Alexander_dead
		set_country_flag = Dudley_Pound_dead
		set_country_flag = Sir_Roger_Backhouse_dead
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_liberal_government = yes
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CAN_Louis_St_Laurent_for_sli
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_liberal_government = yes
				has_country_flag = CAN_lib_ccf_coalition
			}
			add_ideas = CAN_Thomas_C_Douglas_for_sde
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					AND = {
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						NOT = {
							has_country_leader_ideology = authdem_social_credit_subtype
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CAN_Robert_Manion_for_sco
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader_ideology = authdem_social_credit_subtype
					has_country_leader_ideology = social_credit_subtype
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CAN_Chester_Reynolds_for_ade
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GBR = {
					has_country_flag = GBR_Douglas_PM
				}
				has_idea = CAN_CH_Douglas_eco_ade
			}
			remove_ideas = CAN_CH_Douglas_eco_ade
			add_ideas = CAN_WAC_Bennett_eco_ade
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject = no
					OR = {
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						has_government = paternal_autocrat
					}
					has_country_flag = CAN_WMA_absolutism
				}
				country_event = { id = canada.301 days = 3 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject = no
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_country_flag = CAN_absolutism_is_temporary
				}
				country_event = { id = canada.3010 days = 3 }
			}
			else = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					long_name = CAN_social_credit_party_long
					name = CAN_social_credit_party
				}
				set_country_flag = CAN_soccreds_exist
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = canada.427
						days = 11
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = canada.325
				days = 55
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_restored_senate }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = canada.446
					days = 133
					random_days = 44
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = canada.453
				days = 100
				random = 80
			}
		}
	}
}

# Restoring civilian government in Canada
country_event = {
	id = canada.301
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.301" }
	title = canada.301.t
	desc = canada.301.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_parliament1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_subject = no
		OR = {
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			has_government = paternal_autocrat
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.301.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			set_country_flag = CAN_was_authdem
			add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = -0.20 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
			set_country_flag = CAN_was_pataut
			add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = -0.20 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { social_conservative < 0.40 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.10 }
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 12
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		GBR_returning_king_check = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_meighen }
				add_ideas = CAN_Arthur_Meighen_hog_sco
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bracken }
				add_ideas = CAN_John_Bracken_hog_sco
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_RB_Bennett_hog_sco
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CAN_has_exile_govt = yes }
				CAN_add_british_pm_in_exile = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_Sidney_Earle_Smith_for_sco
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bracken }
				add_ideas = CAN_Stephen_Leacock_eco_sco
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_John_Bracken_eco_sco
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_diefenbaker }
				add_ideas = CAN_Gordon_Graydon_sec_sco
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAN_John_Diefenbaker_sec_sco
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = CAN_social_credit_party_long
				name = CAN_social_credit_party
			}
			set_country_flag = CAN_soccreds_exist
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = canada.427
					days = 11
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = CAN_cadets_idea
			remove_ideas = CAN_new_nobility_idea
			remove_ideas = CAN_promoted_english
			remove_ideas = CAN_state_capitalism
			remove_ideas = CAN_anti_syndicalism_decree
			remove_ideas = CAN_national_security_act
			remove_ideas = CAN_canadian_resistance
			remove_ideas = CAN_canadian_resistance2
		}
	}
}

		is_subject = no

			has_government = authoritarian_democrat

		}

		name = canada.301.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = -0.20 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = -0.20 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = -0.20 }

			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = market_liberal

# The Canadian Governor General (fired by UK focus)
country_event = {
	id = canada.302
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.302" }
	title = canada.302.t
	desc = canada.302.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_parliament1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		CAN = {
			is_in_faction_with = GBR
			NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_is_republic }
		}
	}

	option = { # Unite the Thrones
		name = canada.302.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		CAN = {
			country_event = {	
				id = canada.3031
				days = 16
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3038
				days = 2
			}
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3036
				days = 40
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # New King
		name = canada.302.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.05
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = CAN_king_albert_I
			}
			NEE = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Albert I"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = ENT_Albert_Dead }
		}
		CAN = {
			country_event = {	
				id = canada.3039
				days = 16
			}
		}
		CAN_set_king_albert = yes
		GBR = {
			clear_global_event_target = ENT_Prince_Albert_Target
		}
		save_global_event_target_as = ENT_Prince_Albert_Target
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3038
				days = 2
			}
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3036
				days = 40
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # New GG
		name = canada.302.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = canada.303
			days = 3
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_gov_gen
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3038
				days = 2
			}
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3036
				days = 40
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Republic
		name = canada.302.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				check_variable = { CAN_was_king_popularity < 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_referendum
					option = CAN_REFERENDUM_MEMBER_OR_THE_EMPIRE
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = CAN_entente_leadership_unavailable
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_is_republic
		CAN_setup_transitional_committee = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = CAN_republic
		news_event = { id = canada.316 days = 1 }
		set_country_flag = CAN_gov_gen
		country_event = {
			id = canada.3032
			days = 3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3037
				days = 40
			}
		}
	}
}

					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = CAN_suppress_quebecois
						has_completed_focus = CAN_war_measures_act
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = canada.305 days = 8 random = 72 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { CAN_was_king_popularity < 2 } }
				country_event = { id = canada.306 days = 15 random = 72 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = canada.307 days = 15 random = 72 }
			}
			country_event = { id = canada.308 days = 20 random = 72 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = CAN_war_measures_act }
				country_event = { id = canada.309 days = 25 random = 72 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = canada.310 days = 25 random = 72 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# The Referendum
country_event = {
	id = canada.315
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.315" }
	title = canada.315.t
	desc = canada.315.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_subject = no
		CAN_has_elections = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.315.a #Cut ties with the monarchy
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_referendum
					option = CAN_REFERENDUM_MEMBER_OR_THE_EMPIRE
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				check_variable = { CAN_was_king_popularity < 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				check_variable = { CAN_was_king_popularity < 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_completed_focus = CAN_suppress_quebecois
				OR = {
					466 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN }
					468 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN }
					832 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = CAN_was_authdem
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = CAN_was_pataut
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_british_campaign_vote
		clr_country_flag = CAN_was_authdem
		clr_country_flag = CAN_was_pataut
		set_country_flag = CAN_is_republic
		add_political_power = -200
		add_stability = -0.20
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_becomes_republic_tt
		if = {
			limit = { CAF = { is_subject_of = CAN } }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = CAF
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { AST = { is_subject_of = CAN } }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = AST
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NZL = { is_subject_of = CAN } }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = NZL
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CAN_is_republic
			CAN_setup_transitional_committee = yes
			set_cosmetic_tag = CAN_republic
			news_event = { id = canada.316 days = 1 }
			set_country_flag = CAN_gov_gen
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3032
				days = 3
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = canada.3037
					days = 40
				}
			}
			CAN_create_republic = yes
			news_event = { id = canada.316 days = 1 }
		}
		set_global_flag = CAN_left_entente
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.315.b #We are a loyal member of the Empire
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_referendum
					option = CAN_POLITICAL_REPUBLIC
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				check_variable = { CAN_was_king_popularity > 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				check_variable = { CAN_was_king_popularity > 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				check_variable = { CAN_was_king_popularity > 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_completed_focus = CAN_new_quebec_status
				OR = {
					466 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN }
					468 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN }
					832 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_country_flag = CAN_gov_gen_mcnaughton
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = CAN_british_campaign_vote
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_brit_leadership
		clr_country_flag = CAN_british_campaign_vote
		clr_country_flag = CAN_was_authdem
		clr_country_flag = CAN_was_pataut
		set_country_flag = CAN_loyal_to_britain
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = canada.317 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# The Question of Quebec Autonomy
country_event = {
	id = canada.319
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.319" }
	title = canada.319.t
	desc = canada.319.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_quebec2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_subject = no
		CAN_has_elections = yes
		owns_state = 466 #Quebec
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.319.a #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -300
		add_stability = -0.20
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.319.b #Grant them autonomy
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { CAN_provinces = 1 }
		subtract_from_variable = { CAN_current_provinces = 1 }
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.5
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 466 #Quebec
					state = 468 #Saint Lawrence
					state = 683 #New Quebec
					state = 832 #Montreal
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = CAN
			QUE = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		332 = { add_claim_by = QUE }
		QUE = { get_current_government_type = yes }
		puppet = QUE
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
			ENT = { add_to_faction = QUE }
		}
		QUE = {
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				add_political_power = 100
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = KR_close_allies }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = KR_close_allies }
				news_event = { id = canada.320 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.319.c #Full independence
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { CAN_provinces = 1 }
		subtract_from_variable = { CAN_current_provinces = 1 }
		add_political_power = -200
		add_stability = 0.05
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 466 #Quebec
					state = 468 #Saint Lawrence
					state = 683 #New Quebec
					state = 832 #Montreal
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = CAN
			QUE = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		332 = { add_claim_by = QUE }
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = QUE
			relation = docking_rights
			active = yes
		}
		give_guarantee = QUE
		QUE = {
			give_military_access = CAN
			hidden_effect = {
				add_political_power = 100
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = KR_close_allies }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = KR_close_allies }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = CAN
					relation = docking_rights
					active = yes
				}
				news_event = { id = canada.320 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# NEE, Canada said fuck you brit losers, what do we do
country_event = {
	id = canada.3220
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.3220" }
	title = canada.3220.t
	desc = canada.3220.d
	picture = GFX_NEE_new_england

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Canadas our bro
		name = canada.3220.a
		CAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3221
				days = 1
			}
		}

	}
	
	option = { #Fuck u bitchass
		name = canada.3220.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3222
				days = 1
			}
		}

	}
	
	option = { #Fuck all y'all
		name = canada.3220.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		leave_faction = yes
		CAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3222
				days = 1
			}
		}
		GBR = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3222
				days = 1
			}
		}

	}
}

# News: Canada withdraws from the Entente

	id = canada.323
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.323" }
	title = canada.323.t
	desc = canada.323.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_CAN_parliament

	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.323.a
		trigger = { tag = CAN }
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.323.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = ENT
				is_in_faction_with = ENT
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = canada.323.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = CAN
				tag = ENT
				is_in_faction_with = ENT
			}
		}
	}
}

# Canada claims a state
country_event = {
	id = canada.324
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.324" }
	title = canada.324.t
	desc = canada.324.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_army1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.324.a
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = KR_hates_govt }
		if = {
			limit = { gives_military_access_to = FROM }
			FROM = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { gives_military_access_to = ROOT } }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = military_access
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = no
			}
		}
	}
}

#Status of Newfoundland
country_event = {
	id = canada.325
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.325" }
	title = canada.325.t
	desc = canada.325.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFL_commission

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = NFL_was_annexed_by_canada
	}

	option = {
		name = canada.325.a
		trigger = {
			country_exists = GBR
			#GBR = {
			#	is_subject = no
			#}
		}
		NFL = {
			transfer_state = 331
			transfer_state = 332
			add_state_core = 331
			add_state_core = 332
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = NFL_memories_of_the_regiment
				remove_ideas = NFL_reliance_on_canada
				remove_ideas = NFL_bad_economy
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = NFL_Walter_Stanley_Monroe_hog_sco
		}
		NFL = {
			get_current_government_type = yes
		}
		CAN = {
			puppet = NFL
		}
		NFL = {
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
		}
		remove_state_core = 331
		remove_state_core = 332
		subtract_from_variable = { CAN_provinces = 1 }
		subtract_from_variable = { CAN_current_provinces = 1 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.325.b
		add_stability = 0.02
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.325.c
		NFL = {
			transfer_state = 331
			transfer_state = 332
			add_state_core = 331
			add_state_core = 332
			hidden_effect = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				NFL_set_GG_walwyn = yes
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					NFL_James_A_Winter_hog_pau
					NFL_Sir_John_Hope_Simpson_for_pau
					NFL_William_Richard_Howley_eco_pau
					NFL_Thomas_Lodge_sec_pau
				}
				remove_ideas = NFL_memories_of_the_regiment
				remove_ideas = NFL_reliance_on_canada
				remove_ideas = NFL_bad_economy
				NFL = {
					get_current_government_type = yes
				}
				CAN = {
					puppet = NFL
				}
				NFL = {
					restore_previous_government_type = yes
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = canada.3250
			days = 34
		}
		remove_state_core = 331
		remove_state_core = 332
	}
}

#Newfoundland Elections
country_event = {
	id = canada.3250
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.3250" }
	title = canada.3250.t
	desc = canada.3250.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFL_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.3250.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3251
				days = 30
			}
		}
		NFL = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_liberal
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.10
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				NFL_Joey_Smallwood_hog_sli
				NFL_Chesley_William_Carter_for_sli
				NFL_Samuel_J_Hefferton_eco_sli
				NFL_Leonard_Outerbridge_sec_sli
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.3250.b
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.3252
				days = 30
			}
		}
		NFL = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.10
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				NFL_Peter_John_Cashin_hog_sde
				NFL_Malcolm_Mercer_Hollett_for_sde
				NFL_Frank_Fogwill_eco_sde
				NFL_Chesley_Crosbie_sec_sde

		}

country_event = { # Implementing Social Credit
	id = canada.403

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.403.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
		}

		random_owned_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_state = {

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.420" }
	title = canada.420.t
	desc = canada.420.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_douglas_pound

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Nah
		name = canada.420.a
		add_political_power = 20
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.421
				days = 33
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Sure
		name = canada.420.b
		GBR_reset_GB_PM = yes
		add_ideas = CAN_CH_Douglas_lobe_pau
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CAN_CH_Douglas_eco_ade
			}
			remove_ideas = CAN_CH_Douglas_eco_ade
			add_ideas = CAN_WAC_Bennett_eco_ade
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_Douglas_GB_PM
		GBR = {
			set_country_flag = GBR_Douglas_PM
		}
		add_political_power = -20
		
	}
	
	option = { #£
		name = canada.420.c
		GBR_reset_GB_PM = yes
		add_ideas = CAN_Ezra_Pound_lobe_pau
		set_country_flag = CAN_Pound_GB_PM
		GBR = {
			set_country_flag = GBR_Pound_PM
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		
	}
	
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_hargrave

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Sure
		name = canada.421.a
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = -0.02
		GBR_reset_GB_PM = yes
		add_ideas = CAN_John_Hargrave_lobe_pau
		set_country_flag = CAN_Hargrave_GB_PM
		GBR = {
			set_country_flag = GBR_Hargrave_PM
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CAN_John_Hargrave_sec_pau
			}
			remove_ideas = CAN_John_Hargrave_sec_pau
			add_ideas = CAN_Real_Caouette_sec_pau
		}
	}
	
	option = { #No
		name = canada.421.b
		add_stability = 0.02
	}
	
}

country_event = { # Appoint Hargrave
	id = canada.422
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.422" }
	title = canada.422.t
	desc = canada.422.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_hargrave

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Sure
		name = canada.422.b
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = -0.02
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = CAN_John_Hargrave_hog_pau
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_blackmore
			clr_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_caouette
			clr_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_douglas
			clr_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_manning
			set_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_hargrave
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "John Hargrave"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Britain_John_Hargrave.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_social_credit_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "John Hargrave"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Britain_John_Hargrave.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = social_credit_subtype
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					CAN_is_dominion = yes
					NOT = { country_exists = GBR }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = canada.4220
					days = 65
					random_days = 11
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #No
		name = canada.422.a
		add_stability = 0.02
	}
	
}

country_event = { # The Death of William Aberhart
	id = canada.424
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.424" }
	title = canada.424.t
	desc = {
		text = canada.424.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = CAN_William_Aberhart_hog_pau
				has_idea = CAN_Ernest_Manning_hog_ade
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.424.d_2
		trigger = {
			has_idea = CAN_William_Aberhart_hog_pau
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = canada.424.d_3
		trigger = {
			has_idea = CAN_Ernest_Manning_hog_ade
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_aberhart3
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_aberhart }
				clr_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_aberhart
			}
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.424.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = CAN_William_Aberhart_hog_pau
			}
	    }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CAN_soccreds_exist
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_dictatorship
				}
				has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_aberhart
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = canada.426
					days = 11
				}
				clr_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_aberhart
			}
		}
		
		set_country_flag = William_Aberhart_dead
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = CAN_Ernest_Manning_hog_ade
					has_country_flag = CAN_distancing_social_credit
					has_country_flag = CAN_soccred_for_now
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = canada.425
				days = 55
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.424.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CAN_political_path
					option = CAN_POLITICAL_PATH_SOCCRED_PATAUT
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_idea = CAN_William_Aberhart_hog_pau
		}
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = CAN_Ernest_Manning_hog_ade
		set_country_flag = William_Aberhart_dead
		
		set_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_manning
		
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_pataut_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = {
			current_pataut_pop = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat
		}
		set_variable = {
			current_authdem_pop = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = current_pataut_pop
			value = current_authdem_pop
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = current_pataut_pop
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = authdem_social_credit_subtype
		set_country_flag = CAN_authdems_are_social_credit
		set_country_flag = CAN_subtype_change 
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Ernest Manning"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_Ernest_Manning.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_social_credit_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.424.c
		trigger = {
			has_idea = CAN_William_Aberhart_hog_pau
		}
		
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = CAN_JH_Blackmore_hog_ade
		set_country_flag = William_Aberhart_dead
		
		set_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_blackmore
		
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_pataut_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = {
			current_pataut_pop = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat
		}
		set_variable = {
			current_authdem_pop = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = current_pataut_pop
			value = current_authdem_pop
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = current_pataut_pop
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = authdem_social_credit_subtype
		set_country_flag = CAN_authdems_are_social_credit
		set_country_flag = CAN_subtype_change 
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "John Horne Blackmore"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_JH_Blackmore.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authdem_social_credit_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.424.e
		trigger = {
			has_idea = CAN_William_Aberhart_hog_pau
		}
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = CAN_Real_Caouette_hog_pau
		set_country_flag = William_Aberhart_dead
		
		set_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_caouette
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CAN_Real_Caouette_sec_pau
			}
			add_ideas = CAN_Ernest_Manning_sec_ade
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Réal Caouette"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/QUE/Portrait_Quebec_Real_Caouette.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = social_credit_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {
		name = canada.424.f
		trigger = {
			has_idea = CAN_William_Aberhart_hog_pau
			NOT = {
				has_idea = CAN_CH_Douglas_lobe_pau
				country_exists = GBR
			}
		}
	
		set_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_douglas
		
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = CAN_CH_Douglas_hog_ade
		set_country_flag = William_Aberhart_dead
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CAN_CH_Douglas_eco_ade
			}
			remove_ideas = CAN_CH_Douglas_eco_ade
			add_ideas = CAN_WAC_Bennett_eco_ade
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "C. H. Douglas"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Britain_Clifford_Hugh_Douglas.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = social_credit_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.763.e
		trigger = {
			has_idea = CAN_William_Aberhart_hog_pau
			has_country_flag = CAN_technocracy_inc
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_haldeman
		
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = CAN_Joshua_N_Haldeman_hog_pau
		set_country_flag = William_Aberhart_dead
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Joshua N. Haldeman"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_Joshua_N_Haldeman.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = social_credit_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = { # Manning goes SocCon
	id = canada.425
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.425" }
	title = canada.425.t
	desc = canada.425.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_manning3

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #cool
		name = canada.425.a
		clr_country_flag = CAN_soccreds_exist
		clr_country_flag = CAN_soccred_dictatorship
		clr_country_flag = CAN_soccred_leader_manning
		set_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_manning
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bennett
			clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_stevens
			clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_bracken
			clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_diefenbaker
			clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_drew
			clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_manion
			clr_country_flag = CAN_cons_leader_meighen
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_authdem_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = {
			current_soccred_authdem_pop = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat
		}
		set_variable = {
			current_soccon_pop = party_popularity@social_conservative
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = current_soccred_authdem_pop
			value = current_soccon_pop
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = current_soccred_authdem_pop
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pm_is_hos }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Ernest Manning"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_Canada_Ernest_Manning.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = moderate_authoritarianism_subtype
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			long_name = CAN_prog_conservative_party_long
			name = CAN_prog_conservative_party
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			long_name = CAN_prog_conservative_party_long
			name = CAN_prog_conservative_party
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = moderate_authoritarianism_subtype
		set_country_flag = CAN_soccons_are_modauth
		set_country_flag = CAN_subtype_change
	}
}

country_event = { # UK Reclaimed
	id = canada.428
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.428" }
	title = canada.428.t
	desc = canada.428.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GBR_country_parliament

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #cool
		name = canada.428.a
		set_cosmetic_tag = CAN_UK
		set_capital = { state = 126 }
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_british_isles = yes }
			add_core_of = CAN
		}
		set_global_flag = ENT_CAN_REFORMED_UK
		set_variable = { GBR_pw_dev = 20 }
		set_variable = { GBR_legacy_rev = 5 }
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GBR_postwar_devastation }
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GBR_legacy_revolution }
		add_ideas = GBR_postwar_devastation_idea
		add_ideas = GBR_legacy_revolution_idea
		add_ideas = GBR_military_chaos_1
		clr_country_flag = cannot_have_conscription
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_socialist_government = yes 
					is_dynamic_country = no
				}
				ROOT = { embargo_PREV = yes }
			}
			country_event = { id = uk.4 days = 3 } #first Liberty Day
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.2
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.2
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.2
		}
		GBR_recalculate_legacy_revolution = yes
		GBR_recalculate_postwar_devastation = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Edward VIII"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_leader_description = {
				desc = "POLITICS_EDWARD_GBR_DESC"
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "George V"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_leader_description = {
				desc = "POLITICS_GEORGE_GBR_DESC"
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Albert I"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_leader_description = {
				desc = "POLITICS_ALBERT_GBR_DESC"
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Henry IX"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_leader_description = {
				desc = "POLITICS_KING_HENRY_GBR_DESC"
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "George VI"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_leader_description = {
				desc = "POLITICS_KING_GEORGE_GBR_DESC"
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = GBR_british_exile_trait
			}
			remove_unit_leader_trait = GBR_british_exile_trait
		}
		TRM = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_unit_leader_flag = CAN_TRM_expedition_leader }
				set_nationality = GBR
				remove_unit_leader_trait = TRM_british_expeditionary
			}
		}
		remove_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = CAN_brit_govt_exile_idea
		}
		remove_power_balance = { id = CAN_brit_exile_balance }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.453
				days = 100
				random = 80
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.669"}
	title = canada.669.t
	desc = canada.669.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_belize

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {# No
		name = canada.669.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		CAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.670
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {# Yes
		name = canada.669.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		CAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.671
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {# Only if they fuck up Nicaragua
		name = canada.669.c
		trigger = {
			has_war_with = NIC
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = -20
				NIC = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = canada.672
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
}

#####Treaty with Germany#####
country_event = {# Canadian - German Treaty
	id = canada.3060
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.3060"}
	title = canada.3060.t
	desc = canada.3060.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = CAN
		country_exists = ENG
		NOT = { has_war_with = CAN }
	}

	option = {# Accept
		name = canada.3060.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		set_global_flag = CAN_germany_treaty
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CAN }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = CAN_GER_treaty_accept }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = CAN_GER_treaty_accept }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CAN }
			diplomatic_relation = { country = CAN relation = non_aggression_pact }
		}
		CAN = {
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = GER }
				diplomatic_relation = { country = GER relation = non_aggression_pact }
			}
			country_event = { id = canada.3070 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {# Reject
		name = canada.3060.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CAN }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = CAN_GER_treaty_reject }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = CAN_GER_treaty_reject }
		}
		CAN = {
			country_event = { id = canada.3080 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}
country_event = {# Germany accepts treaty
	id = canada.3070
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.3070"}
	title = canada.3070.t
	desc = canada.3070.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.3070.a
		add_stability = 0.08
	}
}
country_event = {# Germany rejects treaty
	id = canada.3080
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.3080"}
	title = canada.3080.t
	desc = canada.3080.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #So be it
		name = canada.3080.a
		add_stability = -0.08

	}
}
country_event = {# Fullfiling the Treaty
	id = canada.3090
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.3090"}
	title = canada.3090.t
	desc = canada.3090.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_global_flag = CAN_germany_treaty
		country_exists = CAN
		NOT = { has_war_with = CAN }
		any_owned_state = {
			is_controlled_by = GER
			is_british_isles = yes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {	days = 5 }

	option = {# Give the Land back
		name = canada.3090.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				126 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Greater London Area
				122 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Wales
				136 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Aberdeenshire
			}
			clr_global_flag = CAN_germany_treaty
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = GER
				is_british_isles = yes
			}
			CAN = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {# We shall not.
		name = canada.3090.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		add_stability = -0.08
		clr_global_flag = CAN_germany_treaty
	}
}

#####Treaty with Portugal#####
country_event = {# Canadian - Portugal Treaty
	id = canada.3000
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.3000"}
	title = canada.3000.t
	desc = canada.3000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept
		name = canada.3000.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		set_global_flag = CAN_portugal_treaty
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = CAN_POR_treaty_accept }
		CAN = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = CAN_POR_treaty_accept } }
		CAN = {
			give_military_access = POR
			give_guarantee = POR
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = POR }
				diplomatic_relation = { country = POR relation = non_aggression_pact }
			}
			country_event = { id = canada.3011 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { #Reject
		name = canada.3000.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = CAN modifier = CAN_POR_treaty_reject }
		CAN = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = CAN_POR_treaty_reject } }
		CAN = { country_event = { id = canada.3020 days = 1 } }

	}
}

		set_global_flag = CAN_canada_controls_shetland
	}
	
	option = {
		name = canada.3056.b
		trigger = {
			tag = ENG
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		navy_experience = -30
	}
}

####Claiming the Oregon territory####
country_event = {# Canada demands the Oregon Territory
	id = canada.2011
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.2011"}
	title = canada.2011.t
	desc = canada.2011.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_oregon

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Cede all territory
		name = canada.2011.a
		ai_chance = { #should be very unlikely to say yes unless they are being attacked.
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				num_of_controlled_states < 4
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			country_event = canada.2012
		}
	}
	option = { #Compromise
		name = canada.2011.b
		ai_chance = { #Should be 4x more likely than full scession, but still fairly unlikely if they aren't under attack.
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				num_of_controlled_states < 3
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			country_event = canada.2013
		}
	}
	option = { #Refuse - Canada invades
		name = canada.2011.c
		ai_chance = { #strongly in favour of rejecting the demand unless under attack
			factor = 70
			modifier = { #If PSA has a guarantee or alliance, rejecting Canada's demand should be a certainty
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					is_in_faction = yes
					any_country = {
						ROOT = { is_guaranteed_by = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				has_war = yes
				tag = CAL
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_war = yes
				tag = USA
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			country_event = canada.2014
		}
	}
}

country_event = {# Cede the Oregon Territory
	id = canada.2012
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.2012"}
	title = canada.2012.t
	desc = canada.2012.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_oregon

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = canada.2012.a
		FROM = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 386 #Washington
						state = 385 #Oregon
						state = 387 #Idaho
					}
					is_controlled_by = FROM
				}
				CAN = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {# Offers a compromise
	id = canada.2013
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.2013"}
	title = canada.2013.t
	desc = canada.2013.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_oregon

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept
		name = canada.2013.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = { has_war = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				CAN = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = AST
						has_war_with = ENG
						has_war_with = GER
						has_war_with = CSA
						has_war_with = USA
						has_war_with = TEX
					}
				}
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			transfer_state = 386 #Washington
			remove_state_claim = 385 #Oregon
			remove_state_claim = 387 #Idaho
		}
		FROM = { country_event = canada.2015 }
	}

	option = { #Reject and declare war
		name = canada.2013.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { has_war = yes }
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

country_event = {# Refuses demands
	id = canada.2014
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event canada.2014"}

	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_oregon

		name = canada.2014.a
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

	desc = canada.2015.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_oregon

		name = canada.2015.a
	}
